## OpenHands Workspace Rules

- The provided working directory is the only submission surface for this evaluation.
- Do not `git clone`, `git init`, or fetch the target repository into the working directory or any of its subdirectories.
- Use MCP to inspect remote code, then create or edit only the files you need directly in the working directory using repository-relative paths.
- The verifier only reads changes from the provided working directory, not from any self-cloned checkout.


# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/argo-cd--v2.13.2`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/argo-cd--v2.13.2$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/argo-cd--v2.13.2` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Onboarding: Argo CD Codebase Orientation

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/argo-cd--v2.13.2 (mirror of argoproj/argo-cd)
**Task Type:** Codebase Orientation (analysis only — no code changes)

## Scenario

You are a new engineer joining a team that works on Argo CD, a declarative GitOps continuous delivery tool for Kubernetes. Your manager has asked you to spend your first day exploring the codebase and answering key orientation questions so you can understand how the system works and start contributing effectively.

## Your Task

Explore the Argo CD codebase and answer the following questions. Write your answers to `/logs/agent/onboarding.md`.

### Questions

1. **Main Entry Points**: Argo CD is a multi-binary system with several core components. Identify the entry points (main functions) for at least 3 of the following components: API server, application controller, repo server, and ApplicationSet controller. For each component, explain its primary responsibility.

2. **Core Packages**: Identify at least 5 key packages and describe what each one is responsible for. Focus on packages that handle: application reconciliation, repository interaction, Kubernetes resource management, API types/CRDs, and utility functions.

3. **Configuration Loading**: How does each component load its configuration? Describe the configuration pipeline: what libraries are used for CLI flags and config files, and where are the main configuration structs defined?

4. **Test Structure**: How are tests organized in this project? Describe at least 3 different types of tests (e.g., unit tests, integration tests, E2E tests). Where do E2E tests live, and what testing frameworks are used?

5. **Application Sync Pipeline**: Trace the path of an Application resource from CRD definition to actual deployment in a Kubernetes cluster. Identify at least 4 stages in this pipeline and name the key packages or files involved at each stage (e.g., CRD types, controller reconciliation loop, repo server manifest generation, kubectl apply).

6. **Adding a New Sync Strategy**: If you needed to add a new sync strategy (e.g., a custom hook or wave behavior), which packages and files would you need to modify? Describe the sequence of changes required to implement a new sync option.

## Output Requirements

Write your answers to `/logs/agent/onboarding.md` with this structure:

```
# Argo CD Codebase Orientation

## 1. Main Entry Points
<Your answer>

## 2. Core Packages
<Your answer>

## 3. Configuration Loading
<Your answer>

## 4. Test Structure
<Your answer>

## 5. Application Sync Pipeline
<Your answer>

## 6. Adding a New Sync Strategy
<Your answer>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT modify any source files
- Do NOT write any code changes
- Your job is exploration and documentation only
- Be specific — include file paths, package names, function names, and struct names where relevant

<ROLE>
Your primary role is to assist users by executing commands, modifying code, and solving technical problems effectively. You should be thorough, methodical, and prioritize quality over speed.
* If the user asks a question, like "why is X happening", don't try to fix the problem. Just give an answer to the question.
</ROLE>

<EFFICIENCY>
* Each action you take is somewhat expensive. Wherever possible, combine multiple actions into a single action, e.g. combine multiple bash commands into one, using sed and grep to edit/view multiple files at once.
* When exploring the codebase, use efficient tools like find, grep, and git commands with appropriate filters to minimize unnecessary operations.
</EFFICIENCY>

<FILE_SYSTEM_GUIDELINES>
* When a user provides a file path, do NOT assume it's relative to the current working directory. First explore the file system to locate the file before working on it.
* If asked to edit a file, edit the file directly, rather than creating a new file with a different filename.
* For global search-and-replace operations, consider using `sed` instead of opening file editors multiple times.
* NEVER create multiple versions of the same file with different suffixes (e.g., file_test.py, file_fix.py, file_simple.py). Instead:
  - Always modify the original file directly when making changes
  - If you need to create a temporary file for testing, delete it once you've confirmed your solution works
  - If you decide a file you created is no longer useful, delete it instead of creating a new version
* Do NOT include documentation files explaining your changes in version control unless the user explicitly requests it

   - API Server: cmd/argocd-server/commands/argocd_server.go → NewCommand()

   - Repo Server: cmd/argocd-repo-server/commands/argocd_repo_server.go → NewCommand()
   - ApplicationSet Controller: cmd/argocd-applicationset-controller/commands/applicationset_controller.go → NewCommand()

3. **How does the Application Controller reconciliation loop work?**
   - ApplicationController struct in controller/appcontroller.go
   - Uses workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface for appRefreshQueue, appOperationQueue, projectRefreshQueue
   - SharedIndexInformer for apps and projects
   - AppStateManager interface (state.go) with CompareAppState() and SyncAppState()
   - CompareWith enum: CompareWithLatestForceResolve(3), CompareWithLatest(2), CompareWithRecent(1), ComparisonWithNothing(0)
   - managedResource struct pairs Target (desired) and Live (actual) with DiffResult
   - SyncAppState() in sync.go: resolves revisions, checks sync windows, calls CompareAppState(), builds sync.SyncContext with options, calls syncCtx.Sync()

---

## Summary of answers

### Q1 — Top-level repository structure
The repo is a **Go monorepo** that compiles to a single binary. `cmd/main.go` dispatches to sub-commands by inspecting `os.Args[0]` (or `ARGOCD_BINARY_NAME`). Key directories: `cmd/` (entry points), `controller/`, `server/`, `reposerver/`, `applicationset/`, `pkg/apis/application/v1alpha1/` (CRD types), `util/` (shared libraries), `common/` (constants), `test/e2e/`.

### Q2 — Four main components and entry points
| Component | Entry point | Role |
|---|---|---|
| API Server | `cmd/argocd-server/commands/argocd_server.go` | gRPC+REST API, auth, RBAC, webhooks |
| Application Controller | `cmd/argocd-application-controller/commands/argocd_application_controller.go` | GitOps reconciliation engine |
| Repo Server | `cmd/argocd-repo-server/commands/argocd_repo_server.go` | Git clone + manifest generation |
| ApplicationSet Controller | `cmd/argocd-applicationset-controller/commands/applicationset_controller.go` | Fleet app generation from templates |

### Q3 — Application Controller reconciliation loop
`ApplicationController` uses `client-go` informers + rate-limiting workqueues. The loop: informer events → `appRefreshQueue` → `CompareAppState()` (diff desired vs live via repo server + cluster cache) → update `Application.Status` → if auto-sync and OutOfSync → `appOperationQueue` → `SyncAppState()` → `sync.NewSyncContext()` + `syncCtx.Sync()` (gitops-engine, wave-by-wave). Source: `controller/appcontroller.go`, `controller/state.go`, `controller/sync.go`, `controller/hook.go`.

### Q4 — Core CRD types
`Application` → `Applicat

How is the top-level repository structured?\n\nThe repository is a **Go monorepo** that compiles into a single binary and dispatches to sub-commands at runtime based on the binary name (or the `ARGOCD_BINARY_NAME` environment variable). The dispatch logic lives in `cmd/main.go`.\n\n### Key top-level directories\n\n| Directory | Purpose |\n|---|---|\n| `cmd/` | Entry-point `main.go` + one sub-directory per component (`argocd-server/`, \u251c\u2500\u2500 \"argocd-server\"                  \u2192 server.NewCommand()\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 \"argocd-application-controller\"  \u2192 appcontroller.NewCommand()\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 \"argocd-cmp-server\"              \u2192 cmpserver.NewCommand()\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 \"argocd\" (default)               \u2192 CLI NewCommand()\n```\n\nAll components share the same compiled binary; Kubernetes deployments use symlinks or `ARGOCD_BINARY_NAME` to select the right sub-command.\n\n---\n\n## Q2. What are the four main components and where do they start?\n\n### 1. API Server\n- **Entry point**: `cmd/argocd-server/commands/argocd_server.go` \u2192 `NewCommand()`\n- **Package**: `github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/server`\n- **Role**: Exposes the gRPC and REST (grpc-gateway) API consumed by the CLI and UI. Handles authentication (Dex/OIDC, local users), RBAC enforcement, webhook ingestion, and proxies requests to the repo server and application controller.\n- **Default port**: 8080 (API), 8083 (metrics)\n- **Key dependencies**: `util/settings` (SettingsManager), `util/db` (ArgoDB), `reposerver/apiclient`, `util/rbac`\n\n### 2. Application Controller\n- **Entry point**: `cmd/argocd-application-controller/commands/argocd_application_controller.go` \u2192 `NewCommand()`\n- **Package**: `github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/controller`\n- **Role**: The core GitOps reconciliation engine. Continuously watches `Application` CRs, compares live cluster state against desired Git state, and drives sync operations. Described in its own command as \"continuously monitors running applications and compares current live state against desired target state.\"\n- **Default port**: 8082 (metrics)\n- **Key dependencies**: `controller/appcontroller.go` (`ApplicationController` struct), `controller/state.go` (`AppStateManager`), `reposerver/apiclient`, `controller/cache` (LiveStateCache), `util/settings`, `util/db`\n\n### 3. Repo Server\n- **Entry point**: `cmd/argocd-repo-server/commands/argocd_repo_server.go` \u2192 `NewCommand()`\n- **Package**: `github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/reposerver/repository`\n- **Role**: Clones Git repositories and generates Kubernetes manifests from them using Helm, Kustomize, plain YAML/Jsonnet, or Config Management Plugins. Exposes a gRPC API consumed by the application controller and API server.\n- **Default port**: 8081 (gRPC), 8084 (metrics)\n- **Key type**: `reposerver/repository.Service` \u2014 holds `gitRepoPaths`, `chartPaths`, `repoLock`, `cache`, `newGitClient`, `newHelmClient`\n\n### 4. ApplicationSet Controller\n- **Entry point**: `cmd/argocd-applicationset-controller/commands/applicationset_controller.go` \u2192 `NewCommand()`\n- **Package**: `github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/applicationset/controllers`\n- **Role**: Watches `ApplicationSet` CRs and generates/manages a fleet of `Application` CRs from parameterized templates. Uses `sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime` (unlike the other components which use raw `client-go` informers).\n- **Key sub-packages**: `applicationset/generators/` (List, Cluster, Git, Matrix, Merge, SCMProvider, PullRequest, ClusterDecision, etc.), `applicationset/services/`, `applicationset/webhook/`\n\n---\n\n## Q3. How does the Application Controller reconciliation loop work?\n\n### Data structures\n\n**`ApplicationController`** (`controller/appcontroller.go`, line 111):\n```go\ntype ApplicationController struct {\n    cache                *appstatecache.Cache\n    kubeClientset        kubernetes.Interface\n    applicationClientset appclientset.Interface\n    appRefreshQueue      workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]  // \"namespace/name\"\n    appComparisonTypeRefreshQueue workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]\n    appOperationQueue    workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]\n    projectRefreshQueue  workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]\n    appInformer          cache.SharedIndexInformer\n    appLister statecache.LiveStateCache\n    statusRefreshTimeout time.Duration         // normal resync period\n    statusHardRefreshTimeout time.Duration     // hard resync period\n    repoClientset        apiclient.Clientset   // gRPC client to repo server\n    db                   db.ArgoDB\n    settingsMgr          *settings_util.SettingsManager\n    clusterSharding      sharding.ClusterShardingCache\n    ...\n}\n```\n\n**`CompareWith`** enum (priority ordering):\n```\nComparisonWithNothing        = 0  // skip comparison, only refresh resource tree\nCompareWithRecent            = 1  // use cached revision from last comparison\nCompareWithLatest            = 2  // fetch latest git revision (cached)\nCompareWithLatestForceResolve = 3 // fetch latest git revision (no cache)\n```\n\n**`managedResource`** (`controller/state.go`):\n```go\ntype managedResource struct {\n    Target *unstructured.Unstructured  // desired state from Git\n    Live   *unstructured.Unstructured  // actual state from cluster\n    Diff   diff.DiffResult\n    Group, Version, Kind, Namespace, Name string\n    Hook   bool\n}\n```\n\n### Reconciliation flow\n\n```\n1. Informers (appInformer, projInformer) watch K8s API server for\n   Application/AppProject add/update/delete events.\n\n2. Events enqueue app keys into appRefreshQueue (rate-limited).\n\n3. Worker goroutines dequeue keys and call processAppRefreshQueueItem():\n   a. Fetch current Application object from lister.\n   b. Determine CompareWith level (forced refresh annotation, auto-sync, etc.).\n   c. Call AppStateManager.CompareAppState():\n      - Calls GetRepoObjs() \u2192 gRPC to repo server \u2192 returns desired manifests.\n      - Fetches live objects from LiveStateCache (cluster cache).\n      - Runs diff (gitops-engine/pkg/diff) between desired and live.\n      - Produces comparisonResult{syncStatus, healthStatus, resources[]}.\n   d. Update Application.Status with sync/health status.\n   e. If auto-sync is enabled and app is OutOfSync \u2192 enqueue into appOperationQueue.\n\n4. Worker goroutines dequeue from appOperationQueue and call processAppOperationQueueItem():\n   a. Calls AppStateManager.SyncAppState(app, operationState):\n      - Resolves ambiguous revisions (branch \u2192 SHA) and pins them in status.\n      - Checks sync windows (blocks sync if window is closed).\n      - Calls CompareAppState() again with noRevisionCache=true.\n      - Builds sync.SyncContext with options derived from SyncOptions flags.\n      - Calls syncCtx.Sync() (gitops-engine) which applies resources wave-by-wave.\n      - Collects per-resource results and writes them to OperationState.\n   b. Updates Application.Status.OperationState.\n\n5. Self-heal: if live state drifts after a successful sync and selfHeal is enabled,\n   the controller re-enqueues the app for another sync after selfHealTimeout.\n```\n\n### Sync pipeline inside `SyncAppState` (`controller/sync.go`)\n\nThe `sync.NewSyncContext` call assembles a set of `SyncOpt` functional options that control the sync engine (from `gitops-engine`):\n\n| Option | Controlled by |\n|---|---|\n| `WithManifestValidation` | `!SyncOptions.HasOption(\"Validate=false\")` |\n| `WithSyncWaveHook` | `delayBetweenSyncWaves` (env `ARGOCD_SYNC_WAVE_DELAY`) |\n| `WithPruneLast` | `SyncOptions.HasOption(\"PruneLast=true\")` |\n| `WithReplace` | `SyncOptions.HasOption(\"Replace=true\")` |\n| `WithServerSideApply` | `SyncOptions.HasOption(\"ServerSideApply=true\")` |\n| `WithResourceModificationChecker` | `SyncOptions.HasOption(\"ApplyOutOfSyncOnly=true\")` |\n| `WithNamespaceModifier` | `SyncOptions.HasOption(\"CreateNamespace=true\")` |\n| `WithPermissionValidator` | Project RBAC enforcement |\n| `WithHealthOverride` | Lua-based custom health checks |\n\nAfter `syncCtx.Sync()` returns, the phase/message/per-resource results are read via `syncCtx.GetState()` and written back to `Application.Status.OperationState.SyncResult`.\n\n### Hook lifecycle (`controller/hook.go`)\n\nHooks are Kubernetes resources annotated with `argocd.argoproj.io/hook: PreSync|Sync|PostSync|PostDelete`. The gitops-engine handles PreSync/Sync/PostSync ordering. Argo CD adds its own `PostDelete` hook support: when an Application is deleted, `executePostDeleteHooks()` creates the hook resources, waits for them to complete, then `cleanupPostDeleteHooks()` deletes them according to their delete policy.\n\n---\n\n## Q4. What are the core CRD types and their key fields?\n\nAll types live in `pkg/apis/application/v1alpha1/types.go` (and `app_project_types.go`, `applicationset_types.go`).\n\n### `Application`\n```go\ntype Application struct {\n    metav1.TypeMeta\n    metav1.ObjectMeta\n    Spec      ApplicationSpec    // desired state\n    Status    ApplicationStatus  // observed state\n    Operation *Operation         // in-progress sync/rollback operation\n}\n```\n\n### `ApplicationSpec`\n```go\ntype ApplicationSpec struct {\n    Source      *ApplicationSource      // single-source          // AppProject name (\"default\" if empty)\n    SyncPolicy  *SyncPolicy\n    IgnoreDifferences IgnoreDifferences // []ResourceIgnoreDifferences\n    Info        []Info\n    RevisionHistoryLimit *int64         // default 10\n}\n```\n\n### `ApplicationSource`\n```go\ntype ApplicationSource struct {\n    RepoURL        string\n    Path           string\n    TargetRevision *ApplicationSourcePlugin\n    Chart          string           // Helm chart name (OCI/Helm repo)\n    Ref            string           // reference name for multi-source\n}\n```\n\nSource-type-specific **`ApplicationSourcePlugin`**: `Name`, `Env`, `Parameters` (`[]ApplicationSourcePluginParameter`)\n\n### `SyncPolicy`\n```go\ntype SyncPolicy struct {\n    Automated   *SyncPolicyAutomated  // enables auto-sync\n    SyncOptions SyncOptions           // []string, e.g. [\"CreateNamespace=true\"]\n    Retry       *RetryStrategy\n    ManagedNamespaceMetadata *ManagedNamespaceMetadata\n}\n\ntype SyncPolicyAutomated struct {\n    Prune      bool  // delete resources removed from Git\n    SelfHeal   bool  // re-sync on live drift\n    AllowEmpty bool  // allow syncing empty source\n}\n\ntype SyncOptions []string  // HasOption(key) / AddOption / RemoveOption helpers\n```\n\nCommon `SyncOptions` string values (constants in `common/common.go`):\n- `\"Validate=false\"` \u2014 skip dry-run validation\n- `\"CreateNamespace=true\"` \u2014 create destination namespace if missing\n- `\"PruneLast=true\"` \u2014 prune resources after all waves complete\n- `\"Replace=true\"` \u2014 use `kubectl replace` instead of `apply`\n- `\"ServerSideApply=true\"` \u2014 use server-side apply\n- `\"ApplyOutOfSyncOnly=true\"` \u2014 only apply out-of-sync resources\n- `\"FailOnSharedResource=true\"` \u2014 fail if resources are owned by another app\n- `\"RespectIgnoreDifferences=true\"` \u2014 apply ignoreDifferences during sync\n\n### `ResourceIgnoreDifferences`\n```go\ntype ResourceIgnoreDifferences struct {\n    Group, Kind, Name, Namespace string\n    JSONPointers      []string  // RFC 6901 JSON Pointer paths\n    JQPathExpressions []string  // jq expressions\n    ManagedFieldsManagers []string  // trusted field managers\n}\n```\n\n### `ApplicationStatus`\nContains: `Resources []ResourceStatus`, `Sync SyncStatus`, `Health HealthStatus`, `History []RevisionHistory`, `Conditions []ApplicationCondition`, `OperationState *OperationState`, `ObservedAt metav1.Time`, `ReconciledAt *metav1.Time`, `SourceType ApplicationSourceType`, `Summary ApplicationSummary`\n\n### `AppProject` (`app_project_types.go`)\nDefines RBAC boundaries: `SourceRepos`, `Destinations`, `ClusterResourceWhitelist/Blacklist`, `NamespaceResourceWhitelist/Blacklist`, `Roles`, `SyncWindows`, `OrphanedResources`, `SignatureKeys`\n\n### `ApplicationSet` (`applicationset_types.go`)\nContains a `Generators []ApplicationSetGenerator` list and a `Template ApplicationSetTemplate`. Generators include: List, Cluster, Git (files/directories), Matrix, Merge, SCMProvider, PullRequest, ClusterDecisionResource, Plugin.\n\n---\n\n## Q5. How does the settings/configuration system work?\n\n### Storage layer: Kubernetes ConfigMaps and Secrets\n\nAll runtime configuration is stored in Kubernetes resources in the Argo CD installation namespace. The canonical names are defined in `common/common.go`:\n\n| K8s Resource | Name | Contents |\n|---|---|---|\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-cm` | Main settings: URL, Dex config, OIDC config, resource customizations, tracking method, kustomize options, anonymous access, etc. |\n| Secret | `argocd-secret` | Sensitive values: server signature (JWT key), TLS cert, webhook secrets, admin password hash |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-rbac-cm` | RBAC policy (`policy.csv`) and default role |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-ssh-known-hosts-cm` | SSH known hosts for Git repos |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-tls-certs-cm` | TLS certificates for Git repos |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-gpg-keys-cm` | GPG public keys for commit verification |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-cmd-params-cm` | Component startup parameters (replaces many CLI flags) |\n| ConfigMap | `argocd-app-controller-shard-cm` | Shard-to-controller mapping for HA |\n\n### `SettingsManager` (`util/settings/settings.go`)\n\n`SettingsManager` watches the above ConfigMaps and Secrets via `client-go` informers and exposes typed accessor methods. It caches the parsed `ArgoCDSettings` struct in memory and notifies subscribers on changes.\n\n### `ArgoCDSettings` struct (key fields)\n\n```go\ntype ArgoCDSettings struct {\n    URL                    string          // external URL (required for SSO)\n    AdditionalURLs         []string\n    DexConfig              string          // Dex YAML config fragment\n    OIDCConfigRAW          string          // OIDC provider config\n    ServerSignature        []byte          // JWT signing key\n    Certificate            *tls.Certificate\n    WebhookGitHubSecret    string\n    WebhookGitLabSecret    string\n    WebhookBitbucketUUID   string\n    WebhookBitbucketServerSecret string\n    WebhookGogsSecret      string\n    WebhookAzureDevOpsUsername string\n    WebhookAzureDevOpsPassword string\n    KustomizeBuildOptions  string\n    AnonymousUserEnabled   bool\n    UserSessionDuration    time.Duration\n    TrackingMethod         string          // \"label\" | \"annotation\" | \"annotation+label\"\n    OIDCTLSInsecureSkipVerify bool\n    AppsInAnyNamespaceEnabled bool\n    ExecEnabled            bool\n    ExecShells             []string\n    InClusterEnabled       bool\n    ImpersonationEnabled   bool\n    ExtensionConfig        map[string]string\n    Secrets                map[string]string  // all argocd-secret keys\n    ...\n}\n```\n\n### `ArgoDB` interface (`util/db/db.go`)\n\n`ArgoDB` abstracts CRUD operations for clusters, repositories, and repository credentials. The implementation stores these as Kubernetes Secrets labeled with `argocd.argoproj.io/secret-type=cluster|repository|repo-creds`. This means cluster credentials and repo credentials are stored as K8s Secrets, not in a separate database.\n\n```go\ntype ArgoDB interface {\n    ListClusters(ctx) (*ClusterList, error)\n    GetCluster(ctx, server string) (*Cluster, error)\n    CreateCluster(ctx, *Cluster) (*Cluster, error)\n    // ... UpdateCluster, DeleteCluster, WatchClusters\n\n    ListRepositories(ctx) ([]*Repository, error)\n    GetRepository(ctx, url, project string) (*Repository, error)\n    // ... CreateRepository, UpdateRepository, DeleteRepository\n\n    // ... repository credentials (CredentialTemplates)\n}\n```\n\n### Environment variables\n\nThe `util/env` package provides typed helpers (`ParseBoolFromEnv`, `ParseInt64FromEnv`, etc.) used throughout the codebase to read env vars with defaults. Many tuning knobs (e.g., `ARGOCD_SYNC_WAVE_DELAY`, `ARGOCD_HELM_ALLOW_CONCURRENCY`) are exposed this way.\n\n### Configuration flow summary\n\n```\nK8s ConfigMap/Secret (argocd-cm, argocd-secret, ...)\n        \u2193  (watched by informers)\n  SettingsManager.cache (ArgoCDSettings)\n        \u2193  (accessor methods)\n  All components: API server, App controller, Repo server\n        \u2193\n  ArgoDB (cluster/repo credentials from labeled K8s Secrets)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Q6. How is the E2E test framework structured?\n\n### Directory layout\n\n```\ntest/e2e/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 fixture/              # shared test infrastructure\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 app/              # fluent DSL for Application lifecycle (Given/When/Then)\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 applicationsets/  # DSL for ApplicationSet tests\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 repos/            # test Git repo helpers\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...               # cluster setup, RBAC helpers, etc.\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 testdata/             # Git repo content used by tests (manifests, charts, etc.)\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 testdata2/            # additional test data\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 app_management_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 hook_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 sync_waves_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 helm_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 kustomize_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 applicationset_test.go\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 ...                   # one file per feature area\n```\n\n### Fluent DSL pattern\n\nTests use a **Given / When / Then** builder pattern imported from `test/e2e/fixture/app`:\n\n```go\nfunc TestPreSyncHookSuccessful(t *testing.T) {\n    Given(t).\n        Path(\"hook\").                          // testdata subdirectory\n    When().\n        PatchFile(\"hook.yaml\", `[...]`).       // mutate test data\n        CreateApp().                           // create Application CR\n        Sync().                                // trigger sync\n    Then().\n        Expect(OperationPhaseIs(OperationSucceeded)).\n        Expect(SyncStatusIs(SyncStatusCodeSynced)).\n        Expect(ResourceHealthIs(\"Pod\", \"pod\", health.HealthStatusHealthy)).\n        Expect(ResourceResultIs(ResourceResult{...}))\n}\n```\n\nThe DSL methods call the real Argo CD API (gRPC/REST) against a live cluster, making these true integration tests.\n\n### Key imports in test files\n\n```go\nimport (\n    . \"github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/pkg/apis/application/v1alpha1\"  // CRD types\n    . \"github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/test/e2e/fixture\"               // shared helpers\n    . \"github.com/argoproj/argo-cd/v2/test/e2e/fixture/app\"           // Given/When/Then DSL\n    . \"github.com/argoproj/gitops-engine/pkg/sync/common\"             // OperationSucceeded, etc.\n    \"github.com/argoproj/gitops-engine/pkg/health\"                    // HealthStatusHealthy, etc.\n    \"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert\"\n    \"github.com/stretchr/testify/require\"\n)\n```\n\nThe dot-imports bring the DSL and type names into scope without qualification, making test code read like a specification.\n\n### Test coverage areas\n\n| Test file | Feature area |\n|---|---|\n| `app_management_test.go` | Core app CRUD, sync, diff |\n| `hook_test.go` | PreSync, Sync, PostSync, PostDelete hooks |\n| `sync_waves_test.go` | Sync wave ordering, degraded app recovery |\n| `app_autosync_test.go` | Automated sync, self-heal |\n| `helm_test.go` | Helm chart rendering, parameters, OCI |\n| `kustomize_test.go` | Kustomize overlays, images, patches |\n| `applicationset_test.go` | ApplicationSet generators and templating |\n| `cluster_generator_test.go` | Cluster generator |\n| `git_test.go` | Git operations, submodules, GPG |\n| `hook_test.go` | Sync hooks lifecycle |\n| `project_management_test.go` | AppProject RBAC |\n| `repo_management_test.go` | Repository CRUD |\n| `sync_options_test.go` | SyncOptions flags |\n| `selective_sync_test.go` | Selective resource sync |\n| `pruning_required_test.go` | Prune behavior |\n| `notification_test.go` | Notification triggers |\n| `diff_test.go` | Diff display |\n| `declarative_test.go` | Declarative app management |\n\n### Running E2E tests\n\nE2E tests require a running Kubernetes cluster with Argo CD installed. They are gated by build tags and environment variables set up by the test fixture's `TestMain`. Individual test files can be run with:\n\n```bash\ngo test ./test/e2e/ -run TestPreSyncHookSuccessful -v -timeout 120s\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key third-party dependencies\n\n| Package | Role |\n|---|---|\n| `github.com/argoproj/gitops-engine` | Core diff, sync, health, and cluster cache logic |\n| `github.com/spf13/cobra` | CLI framework for all component commands |\n| `github.com/sirupsen/logrus` | Structured logging throughout |\n| `k8s.io/client-go` | Kubernetes API client, informers, workqueues |\n| `sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime` | Used by ApplicationSet controller |\n| `google.golang.org/grpc` | Inter-component communication (controller \u2194 repo server) |\n| `github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway` | REST-to-gRPC transcoding for the API server |\n| `github.com/go-git/go-git` | Git operations in the repo server |\n| `helm.sh/helm/v3` | Helm chart rendering |\n| `sigs.k8s.io/kustomize` | Kustomize rendering |\n| `github.com/google/go-jsonnet` | Jsonnet rendering |\n| `github.com/redis/go-redis` | Redis cache (app state, repo cache) |\n| `github.com/stretchr/testify` | Test assertions |\n| `github.com/open-policy-agent/opa` | RBAC policy evaluation |\n| `github.com/dexidp/dex` | Bundled OIDC/SSO provider |\n",
